  select * from emp, dept;
 
 
  select * from emp, dept joining condition;
  
  
  select * from emp t1, dept t2 where t1.deptno=t2.deptno;
  
  
  
  select * from menucard, softdrink;
  
  select * from menucard cross join softdrink;
  
  
  select ename, job, sal, t1.deptno, t2.deptno, dname, loc from emp t1, dept t2 where t1.deptno=t2.deptno;
  
  select * from emp t1 inner join dept t2 on t1.deptno=t2.deptno;
  
  select * from emp t1 natural join dept t2;
  
  select * from emp t1 simple join dept t2 using(deptno);
  
							   L    R
  select ename, deptno.* from emp right outer join dept using(deptno);
